# Where parallel-blas beats epopenblas

Threshold: par/ep ≤ 0.909× wall time (par ≥ 10% faster; anything larger is sub-noise on these benches). Values are ns/call, smaller = faster.
Same-OMP comparison only. Source: `cmp5.tsv` (8702 rows).
